# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="58cf4-102">.NET Framework에서 사용되지 않는 멤버</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="58cf4-102">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="58cf4-103">이 문서는 .NET Framework 4.5 이상 버전에서 사용되지 않은 형식 멤버를 나열합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="58cf4-103">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="58cf4-104">형식 멤버는 어셈블리로 그룹화됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="58cf4-104">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="58cf4-105">사용되지 않는 형식의 멤버는 이 문서에 나열되지 않습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="58cf4-105">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="58cf4-106">사용되지 않는 형식 목록은 [사용되지 않는 형식](obsolete-types.md)을 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="58cf4-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>

> |<xref:Microsoft.Build.BuildEngine.Engine?displayProperty=nameWithType>|<xref:Microsoft.Build.BuildEngine.Engine.%23ctor%28System.String%29>|<span data-ttu-id="58cf4-1134">단순히 .NET Framework 위치를 <xref:Microsoft.Build.BuildEngine.Engine.BinPath%2A>로 전달하는 경우 매개 변수가 없는 <xref:Microsoft.Build.BuildEngine.Engine.%23ctor?displayProperty=nameWithType> 생성자로 변경하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="58cf4-1134">If you were simply passing in the .NET Framework location as the <xref:Microsoft.Build.BuildEngine.Engine.BinPath%2A>, just change to the parameterless <xref:Microsoft.Build.BuildEngine.Engine.%23ctor?displayProperty=nameWithType> constructor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="58cf4-1135">그렇지 않으면 레지스트리 또는 구성 파일에서 사용자 지정 도구 집합을 정의하거나 엔진의 <xref:Microsoft.Build.BuildEngine.ToolsetCollection?displayProperty=nameWithType>에 요소를 추가할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="58cf4-1135">Otherwise, you can define custom toolsets in the registry or configuration file, or add elements to the Engine's <xref:Microsoft.Build.BuildEngine.ToolsetCollection?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="58cf4-1136">그런 다음 <xref:Microsoft.Build.BuildEngine.Engine.%23ctor?displayProperty=nameWithType> 또는 <xref:Microsoft.Build.BuildEngine.Engine.%23ctor%28Microsoft.Build.BuildEngine.ToolsetDefinitionLocations%29?displayProperty=nameWithType> 생성자를 대신 사용하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="58cf4-1136">Then use either the <xref:Microsoft.Build.BuildEngine.Engine.%23ctor?displayProperty=nameWithType> or <xref:Microsoft.Build.BuildEngine.Engine.%23ctor%28Microsoft.Build.BuildEngine.ToolsetDefinitionLocations%29?displayProperty=nameWithType> constructor instead.</span></span>|
